In recent years, the company did not publish relevant ESG reports.The company has not established a board to oversee ESG issues.The company lacks an environmental policy.The company has not established standards to guide the management of social supply chain issues.The social supply chain standard lacks direction on managing forced and child labour.There is no evidence to suggest the company has a whistleblower programme.

In recent years, the company did not publish relevant ESG reports.Evidence suggests there is no board level oversight for ESG issues.A weak environmental policy is in place.The company does not disclose any social supply chain standards.The social supply chain standard lacks direction on managing forced and child labour.There is no evidence to suggest the company has a whistleblower programme.
